### ENTRY: BINARY-c9ba3953-6d8d-4bfd-93f5-55682f6fec13

- bytes: 6286
- crc32: `212508e3`
- decoded_as: `utf-8`

````text
<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>

<mdOwnedViews>
	<mdElement elementClass='DiagramFrame' xmi:id='_17_0_2_3_16a50426_1368762637648_776214_13244'>
		<elementID xmi:idref='_17_0_2_3_16a50426_1368762548264_890057_13219'/>
		<geometry>5, 5, 764, 555</geometry>
		<compartment compartmentID='TAGGED_VALUES'/>
		<mdOwnedViews/>
	</mdElement>
	<mdElement elementClass='TextBox' xmi:id='_17_0_2_3_16a50426_1368768095944_292963_28362'>
		<properties>
			<mdElement elementClass='BooleanProperty'>
				<propertyID>HTML_TEXT</propertyID>
				<propertyDescriptionID>HTML_TEXT_DESCRIPTION</propertyDescriptionID>
				<value xmi:value='true'/>
			</mdElement>
		</properties>
		<geometry>203, 42, 546, 470</geometry>
		<mdOwnedViews/>
		<text>&lt;html&gt;
  &lt;head&gt;
		&lt;style&gt;
			p {padding:0px; margin:0px;}
		&lt;/style&gt;
	&lt;/head&gt;
  &lt;body&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;font style=&quot;font-size:18pt&quot; color=&quot;#970035&quot;&gt;Introduction to Forward Contract&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;font style=&quot;font-size:18pt&quot;&gt;&lt;/font&gt;
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
To provide brief background about forward contract, assume that both parties can borrow and lend at risk free interest rate and the transaction cost is zero, the forward contract is the contract which obligates the parties entering into the contract to buy or to sell specified asset at the price specified in the contract at the end of the contract. The party which is obligated to buy the underlying asset in the future, is said to be long, and the party which is obligated to sell the underlying asset in the future, is said to be short.
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
Normally, at the initiation of the contract the value of the contract is zero. Forward price&amp;#160;is the price of the underlying asset specified in the contract. Spot price&amp;#160;is the present price of the underlying asset. The forward price is the spot price multiply with the risk free interest rate during the period of the contract. In other word, the forward price should equal to the spot price plus the return from lending the money at the quantity of spot price at the risk free rate for the period of forward contract.
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
As the time passes, the value of the underlying asset may change. As a result the value of the contract is not zero for either side. However, the sum of the value of the contract of both long and short side is zero, in other word, this is the zero sum game. The value of the long side is the spot price minus the present value of the forward price because the long side has obligation to buy the underlying asset at forward price and can sell asset at the spot price. The value of the short side is the present value of the forward price minus spot price because the short side has obligation to sell the underlying asset at the forward price and can buy asset at the spot price. The present value of the forward price is the forward price divided by the risk free interest rate for the period until the contract ends. The equation for value of the long and short sides of forward contract are specified below.
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;V (long side) = S-F/[(1+r)^(t/365)]
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;V (short side) = F/[(1+r)^(t/365)] - S
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
where V is the value of the contract
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;S is the spot price of the underlying asset
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;r &amp;#160;is the risk free interest rate
    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;t &amp;#160;is the day until the end of the contract

    &lt;/p&gt;

  &lt;/body&gt;
&lt;/html&gt;
</text>
	</mdElement>
	<mdElement elementClass='RectangularShape' xmi:id='_17_0_2_3_16a50426_1368768163021_794482_28364'>
````
